                            "content": "<span>Trypophobia Penyakit Takut Lubang \u2013 Fobia merupakan ketakutan yang dialami oleh seseorang terhadap suatu obyek yang menimbulkan dampak nyata. Selama ini mungkin jenis fobia seperti hydrophobia atau ornithophobio sudah akrab di telinga. Namun pernahkah anda mendengar trypophobia? Jenis fobia yang satu ini merupakan ketakutan ketika melihat lubang kecil yang jumlahnya banyak. Kenapa hal tersebut bisa terjadi dan bagaimana cara mengobatinya? simak ulasan siputnews berikut ini<br \/><br \/><\/span><span><strong>Gejala Trypophobia<\/strong><br \/>Seseorang yang mengalami trypophobia akan merasa gelisah dan bahkan sampai mengalami gatal di sekujur tubuh ketika melihat obyek yang terdapat banyak lubang pada permukaanya seperti spons, sumsung tulang, biji bunga teratai dan lainya. Pada umumnya penderita trypophobia akan mengalami dua kemungkinan yakni berani melihat kemudian melupakanya namun ada pula yang merasa pusing dan eneg setelah melihat lubang tersebut.Berikut ini reaksi yang dialami seseorang yang mengalami fobia seperti trypophobia:<\/span>Panik dan mengalami rasa takut berlebihan saat berhadapan dengan sumber rasa takutnya.Mengalami cemas dan akan berdampak pada organ tubuh yang tidak berfungsi secara optimal.Mengeluarkan keringat, jantung berdegub kencang, panik, ceas dan bahkan sulit bernafas.Pada penderita anak-anak akan tantrum dan terus menangis.<span><strong>Penyebab Trypophobia<\/strong><br \/>Sampai saat ini belum diketahui penyebab fobia yang cukup aneh tersebut. Beberapa kalangan meyakini bahwa\u00a0Trypophobia sudah dialami sejak anak-anak. Kemungkinan besar yang terjadi adalah mengalami traumatis saat memasuki tahap awal kehidupan. Karena belum diketahui asal-usulnya hingga detik ini belum ada semacam tes atau diagnosa untuk memeriksa fobia ini.<br \/><br \/><\/span><span><strong>Pengobatan Trypophobia<\/strong><br \/>Pada dasarnya tidak semua fobia membutuhkan pengobatan. Hanya saja jika berdampak pada kehidupan sehari-hari maka disarankan untuk melakukan terapi untuk mengatasi ketakutan si penderita. karena Trypophobia belum diketahui secara pasti penyebabnya maka pengobatan yang bisa dilakukan adalah dengan cara konsultasi neurolinguistik, perilaku kognitif, dan konsultasi psikolog. Terapi dengan cara hipnoterapi, terapi perilaku serta konseling sudah terbukti efektif untuk mengobati penderita fobia. Hal ini dikarenakan sebagian besar fobia terjadi karena masalah emosional. Baca juga\u00a0phobia aneh\u00a0lainya.<\/span>",

Do you worry about spiders every time you go into the bathroom? Would you rather walk up 100 steps than get into a lift? If the answer is \u2018yes\u2019 to any of these or similar questions, you may have a phobia!<br \/>\nIf you have a phobia, don\u2019t worry. You are not alone. It\u2019s estimated that about 20% of the world\u2019s population have a phobia about something.  Did you know that some people have a fear of clowns? Can you believe that some people are afraid of fish and that others are scared of garlic? Then there\u2019s a fear of falling in love, the fear of rain, the fear of the moon, and the fear of the starts! However, they cannot control their fears. When some people think about the object of their phobia, their heart starts beating very quickly and they find it difficult to breath. This a natural reaction to fear, but it can make life difficult if it happens all the time.<br \/>\nSo if you have a phobia, what can you do about it? In some cases, you can simply avoid the situation. If you have a fear of heights, don\u2019t climb the mountain! However, in other cases, it\u2019s not so easy.                         "content": "PREDIKSI SOAL TES UM UGM 2016     We often think it very funny if a film shows a women or a girl screaming and running in fight at the sight of a mouse or cockroach. But we don\u2019t consider our own little, secret fears a laughing matter. Perhaps you shiver at the sight of snake or an eel, cannot bear to hear the sound of jagged metal rubbing against metal, or feel uneasy in a lift. Fortunately, most of us suffer only a mild from of fright about certain things. According to psychiatrists, this is quite normal.<br \/>\nIt becomes a problem only when the fear develops into mental condition that affects all aspects of person\u2019s life. Studies of thousands of people with an abnormal dread show that every time they think about - or come into contact with - the subject of their fear, they show all the physical signs of a person who is facing serious danger : a racing heart, dry mouth, cold sweat, and weak knees.<br \/>\nDoctor and psychiatrists welcome publicity about phobias, for this help to convince their patients that their fears are not unique. It reassures the patients to know that there are other people who are afraid of the same thing, and it makes the patients more willing to try to understand what is causing their fear. Once they realize what in their subconscious is causing their fear, they are half-way to being cured. Psychiatrist believe that these unreasonable fears are caused by deep-seated reasons, perhaps a terrifying experience during childhood.<br \/>\nOne typical case was Mrs. Mary Bachelor, a London housewife who suffered from agoraphobia (fears of open spaces). For twenty-three years, she remains indoors. Following publicity about other agoraphobia cases, she was persuaded to go out for the first time to watch her son perform with a pop group.<br \/>\nMost of us suffer from claustrophobia (fear of being in closed areas) in mild way, but the real sufferers go about in great fear of being trapped without escape in a lift, in a packed train or in an aircraft. Altogether, there are a hundred and thirty phobias listed in the medical dictionary, ranging from acrophobia (fear of heights) to xenophobia (morbid dislike of foreigner). Some phobias are very odd indeed, There are cases of people who turn cold with terror at the sight of a cabbage leaf, run away in fright at the sight of a bird or faint when they hear a dog bark. There was even a man who refused to eat anything that he knew had been touched by someone who had handled matches.    \u201cdeep-seated reason\u201d (line ...) most likely means reasons that are___ A. Long forgotten<br \/>\nB. Difficult to choose<br \/>\nC. Not easy to handle<br \/>\nD. Difficult to realize<br \/>\nE. Flexible to charge",

                        "content": "PREDIKSI SOAL TES UM UGM 2016     We often think it very funny if a film shows a women or a girl screaming and running in fight at the sight of a mouse or cockroach. But we don\u2019t consider our own little, secret fears a laughing matter. Perhaps you shiver at the sight of snake or an eel, cannot bear to hear the sound of jagged metal rubbing against metal, or feel uneasy in a lift. Fortunately, most of us suffer only a mild from of fright about certain things. According to psychiatrists, this is quite normal.<br \/>\nIt becomes a problem only when the fear develops into mental condition that affects all aspects of person\u2019s life. Studies of thousands of people with an abnormal dread show that every time they think about - or come into contact with - the subject of their fear, they show all the physical signs of a person who is facing serious danger : a racing heart, dry mouth, cold sweat, and weak knees.<br \/>\nDoctor and psychiatrists welcome publicity about phobias, for this help to convince their patients that their fears are not unique. It reassures the patients to know that there are other people who are afraid of the same thing, and it makes the patients more willing to try to understand what is causing their fear. Once they realize what in their subconscious is causing their fear, they are half-way to being cured. Psychiatrist believe that these unreasonable fears are caused by deep-seated reasons, perhaps a terrifying experience during childhood.<br \/>\nOne typical case was Mrs. Mary Bachelor, a London housewife who suffered from agoraphobia (fears of open spaces). For twenty-three years, she remains indoors. Following publicity about other agoraphobia cases, she was persuaded to go out for the first time to watch her son perform with a pop group.<br \/>\nMost of us suffer from claustrophobia (fear of being in closed areas) in mild way, but the real sufferers go about in great fear of being trapped without escape in a lift, in a packed train or in an aircraft. Altogether, there are a hundred and thirty phobias listed in the medical dictionary, ranging from acrophobia (fear of heights) to xenophobia (morbid dislike of foreigner). Some phobias are very odd indeed, There are cases of people who turn cold with terror at the sight of a cabbage leaf, run away in fright at the sight of a bird or faint when they hear a dog bark. There was even a man who refused to eat anything that he knew had been touched by someone who had handled matches.    The following statements may be the purposes of the writer in writing the text, EXCEPT___<br \/>\nA. To explain the causes of different kinds of phobias<br \/>\nB. To convince people about the importance of publicity about phobias C. To inform people how to overcome their abnormal fears<br \/>\nD. To persuade people with abnormal fears to talk to psychiatrist<br \/>\nE. To inform people about different kinds of phobias<br \/>",

Pulau yang terdiri\natas dua kecamatan, Sangkapura dan Tambak ini sungguh kaya\nobjek wisata. Salah satu yang dituju adalah Pantai Tanjung Anyar\ndi Dusun Tenggen, Desa Lebak, Kecamatan Sangkapura.\nDi Tanjung Anyar terdapat juga kampung nelayan yang\ndihuni sekitar 300 penduduk. Di sepanjang pantainya terdapat\npohon-pohon kelapa dan beberapa pohon besar berbagai jenis.\nKeindahan Pantai Tanjung Anyar akan lebih terasa pada senja\nmenjelang matahari terbenam. Suguhan kesenian tradisional\noleh penduduk dan sajian berbagai jenis ikan laut bakar\nmelengkapi keindahan itu.\nDi bawah salah satu pohon besar terdapat makam yang\npanjangnya sekitar 12 meter sehingga dikenal sebagai makam\npanjang atau dalam bahasa setempat disebut jherat lanjheng.\nTidak jauh dari makam itu juga ada makam lagi dengan panjang\nsekitar 9 meter. Kedua makam itu diyakini sebagai makam dari\nDora dan Sembada, dua pembantu setia Prabu Aji Saka. Aji Saka\nsendiri adalah raja di Jawa dari abad ke-6 Masehi yang\nmengalahkan Prabu Dewatacengkar, penguasa Kerajaan\nMedang.\nDi antara kedua makam pembantunya tersebut, Aji Saka\nmembuat prasasti di atas batu besar dalam huruf Jawa Kuno.\nTulisan di prasasti itu yang dianggap sebagai asal dari huruf-\nhuruf Jawa Kuno atau dikenal sebagai hanacaraka. Sayangnya,\nbatu prasasti tersebut sudah dihancurkan penduduk untuk\ndijadikan fondasi jembatan di desa.\nSelain Tanjung Anyar, terdapat juga Danau Kastoba di Desa\nPromaan. Perjalanan ke Desa Promaan ditempuh dalam satu\njam dari Sangkapura melalui jalan lingkar utama Bawean.\nSesampai di Desa Promaan, kendaraan harus melintasi jalan desa\nsampai ke Dusun Candi yang menjadi gerbang ke Danau\nKastoba. Di dusun itu ada bangunan lumbung padi dari kayu\nyang biasa disebut durung-durung di depan tiap rumah\npenduduk.\nDanau itu berada di Cagar Alam Pulau Bawean, di tengah-\ntengah pulau dengan ketinggian 400 meter di atas permukaan\nlaut. Danau Kastoba luasnya sekitar dua kilometer persegi.\ndengan kedalaman 147 meter. Belum adanya jalan yang\nmengelilingi danau membuat pemandangan benar-benar masih\nalami. Nama Kastoba diambil dari nama pohon kastuba (Eu-\n<em>phorbia<\/em> pulcherrima) yang dulu banyak tumbuh di sana.\nBeberapa ekor burung belibis liar yang berenang di tepi danau\nlangsung terbang menjauh saat kami datang. Warga setempat menyebutkan, warna air danau bisa\nberubah menjadi tiga warna, yaitu merah, hijau, dan seperti\nberminyak. Adanya aroma belerang di sekitar danau juga\nmengindikasikan bahwa danau itu dulunya adalah kawah\ngunung berapi. Spesies yang berbentuk cocok untuk taman\u00a0tropis\u00a0kering dan beriklim sedang.\u00a0Getah susu\u00a0Euphorbia\u00a0dapat menyebabkan iritasi pada kulit, dan ketidaknyamanan parah jika tertelan.<\/p><span><br \/>Semoga membantu dan bermanfaat<\/span>",
